				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<h1 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Streamline Public Sector Purchasing with Government Procurement Software</h1>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-0a34379 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="0a34379" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;ekit_we_effect_on&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">SOVRA's configurable, compliance-driven platform modernizes procurement by streamlining sourcing, contracts, and supplier engagement—reducing administrative burden, increasing competition, and delivering better results for agencies and communities.</h2>				</div>
